# Beta Conversations Operations \{#beta/conversations\}

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/conversations \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list\}

_List all created conversations._

Retrieve a list of conversation entities sorted by creation time.

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/conversations \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start\}

_Create a conversation and append entries to it._

Create a new conversation, using a base model or an agent and append entries. Completion and tool executions are run and the response is appended to the conversation.Use the returned conversation_id to continue the conversation.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\} \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append\}

_Append new entries to an existing conversation._

Run completion on the history of the conversation and the user entries. Return the new created entries.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

</SectionTitle>

##### type \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+request+completion_args+CompletionArgs+response_format+ResponseFormat+type\}

</Property>

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\}/history \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history\}

_Retrieve all entries in a conversation._

Given a conversation_id retrieve all the entries belonging to that conversation. The entries are sorted in the order they were appended, those can be messages, connectors or function_call.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

### Parameters \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history+parameters\}

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content" variant="top-level">

##### conversation\_id <Pill variant="warning">required</Pill> \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history+parameters\}

</SectionContent>

</Section>

<TabbedSection>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\}/messages \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_messages\}

_Retrieve all messages in a conversation._

Given a conversation_id retrieve all the messages belonging to that conversation. This is similar to retrieving all entries except we filter the messages only.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content" variant="top-level">

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\}/restart \{#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_restart\}

_Restart a conversation starting from a given entry._

Given a conversation_id and an id, recreate a conversation from this point and run completion. A new conversation is returned with the new entries returned.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">
